    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

<span id="freeTextContainer9801990157840342419">J.K. Rowling's screenwriting debut is captured in this exciting hardcover edition of the Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them screenplay.<br/><br/>When Magizoologist Newt Scamander arrives in New York, he intends his stay to be just a brief stopover. However, when his magical case is misplaced and some of Newt's fantastic beasts escape, it spells trouble for everyone…<br/><br/>Fantastic Be</span>
  <span id="freeText9801990157840342419" style="display:none">J.K. Rowling's screenwriting debut is captured in this exciting hardcover edition of the Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them screenplay.<br /><br />When Magizoologist Newt Scamander arrives in New York, he intends his stay to be just a brief stopover. However, when his magical case is misplaced and some of Newt's fantastic beasts escape, it spells trouble for everyone…<br /><br />Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them marks the screenwriting debut of J.K. Rowling, author of the beloved and internationally bestselling Harry Potter books. Featuring a cast of remarkable characters, this is epic, adventure-packed storytelling at its very best.<br /><br />Whether an existing fan or new to the wizarding world, this is a perfect addition to any reader's bookshelf.</span>

It's a bit more than just a scrip. It comes a bit closer to being an actual book than the cursed child was. <br />There is also the little textbook from the hogwarts library that also called fantastic beast and where to find them .It's a really cute book.<br />Anyhow I think they'll release all the screenplays of the future movies as well :) Atleast I really hope they do.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>

  <span id="freeText10972415005335608093" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1481298129i/21409293._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>A New Wizarding World saga precedes Harry Potter's<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479406989i/21187480._SY540_.png" width="450" height="503" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Fantastic New World<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462475011ra/19002635.gif" width="450" height="182" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Fantastic Characters;<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479409977i/21187836._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="236" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Beasts-Nerd Hufflepuff Magizoologist<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479409977ra/21187837.gif" width="450" height="180" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Amazing resourceful Sisters<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479409977ra/21187838.gif" width="450" height="187" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479411024ra/21187954.gif" width="450" height="231" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>With a funny <s>Muggle</s> No-Maj character<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1473184745ra/20423481.gif" width="450" height="236" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>&amp; Power hungry men<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479411701ra/21188019.gif" width="450" height="171" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And a Suitcase,<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462475193ra/19002665.gif" width="450" height="180" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462475989ra/19002795.gif" width="450" height="183" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Full of Beasts..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462475989ra/19002796.gif" width="450" height="252" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479412058ra/21188051.gif" width="450" height="252" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>FANTASTIC BEASTS<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479492189ra/21198056.gif" width="450" height="186" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Set Loose in 1920s New York<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462475989ra/19002797.gif" width="450" height="186" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>FIND THEM ALL<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1480815351i/21353423._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="270" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>In a thrilling Fantastic Cinematic experience, chilling Soundtrack mixing Hedwig theme with Saw’s Hello Zepp, comes this Fantastic Story<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479949246i/21255981._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="312" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Written by the Queen of Magic, expanding the Huge World she created, that's hidden among us.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462476833ra/19002926.gif" width="450" height="281" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Wizarding World.<br>With its Fantastic Beasts.. and Where to Find Them.<br><blockquote><b>“they’re currently in alien terrain, surrounded by millions of the most vicious creatures on the planet.<br>Humans.”</b></blockquote>
<br>~~~~~~~~~~~<blockquote><u>The Story &amp; Setting</u></blockquote>
<img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479479991ra/21195602.gif" width="450" height="180" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></b><br>The Story “the Plot of the Movie” is a bit simple, even more than Harry Potter's first book.<br>I was expecting some<i> Prisoner of Azkaban </i>mystery and multi-layers twists.. but here is way simpler plot.. Rich World, yes..but not strong plot.<br><br>Don't get me wrong, I LOVED IT, <b>It's more mature, adult characters now in the leading role, huger world.. and it's still rich enough and entertaining.</b><br>But the more I think of it, it felt like mostly grabbed its richness of the World we already know, and the history of it which we already get a glimpse before.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479479991i/21195603._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="236" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yet, it is here more detailed and it's still amazingly "Fantastically" entertaining and magical in itself.<br><br>Stretching the Wizarding World History both in location and Time.. <br>New York, the 1920s, after the Great War, in the fast changing city, with its new inventions, the prohibited gigglewaters, speakeasy raids..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479493832ra/21198354.gif" width="450" height="180" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And where even the Magical Laws of secrecy in its worst, not even allowing to befriend the No-Maj .. and the No-Maj suspicious and hater of Wizarding World at its peak.<br>All Because of one Notorious Dark Wizard who terrorizing the both worlds..and has as much followers around the world who just helping his cause..<br>Grindelwald. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479493147i/21198258._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="281" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But since he's mostly -may be- not a major here, let's focus on <b>Newt Scamander</b> and the rest of.. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <u>The Characters</u>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>He's this young Magizoologist, the Fantastic Beasts Nerd, comes from England to New York for a certain Beasts-Related mission... in New York where they have no tolerance for Magical "Fantastic" Beasts allowed, they even can kill them to rid of them once and for all..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479493832i/21198355._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="666" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>I just adore how he's so "dorky" in a way, his love for his beasts really remarkable.</i><blockquote>
  <b>NEWT<br>I’ve just completed a year in the field. I’m writing a book about magical creatures.<br>TINA<br>Like—an extermination guide?<br>NEWT<br>No. A guide to help people understand why we should be protecting these creatures instead of killing them.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>But his insignificant misfortune encounter with a very funny, average poor <s>Muggle</s> No-Maj sets a Huge trouble.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479493832i/21198356._SY540_.jpg" width="449" height="665" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Did I tell you that Wizarding world in America doesn't at all collaborations with No-Maj? But come on, you can't easily have enough of this very fun man. and so glad that the story involve a Muggle in a big role this time.</i><br><br>And there's this misfortune Auror, <b>Tina </b>who tries to investigate his mysterious Case of Beasts.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479493832i/21198357._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="667" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But find herself and her extraordinary beautiful charming mind reader sister <b>Queenie</b> getting involved into this huge mess. Finding the Fantastic Beasts..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479494376i/21198415._SY540_.jpg" width="449" height="665" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>Okay, she's my best character here... I love her so much, and The whole movie I been wondering -will they stay together till the end of series? specially Queenie and Jacob "the no-maj" - which heavily reminded me with Strike and Robin relation in a way.</i><b> I mean, it's like He is her Fantastic Beast in a way, and so She is his Fantastic Beast too.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479746658ra/21230953.gif" width="450" height="187" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></b><br><br>All that while in the background, the hatred between some Witch hunters ..Those who hate the others just because they're different..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479495134i/21198493._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="666" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>..those who beside that felt oppressed, hated and looked at lowly..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479495134i/21198494._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="667" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And, on the other side.. Wizards who make stern laws...<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479495134i/21198495._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="666" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>and those who save the law by looking for dark powers..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479495155i/21198497._SY540_.jpg" width="449" height="665" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>..Dark powers that rising in a dangerous deathly political game effects both our World and the Wizarding World.<br><br>It's diversity of characters, with depth analysis of evil nature, prejudices, oppression and locking oneself in a closet while forcing others do as well.. <br><br>And, my God can't say more.. the characters are awesome, more than awesome. Rowling really mastering that.<br><b>~~~~~~~~~~~~<blockquote><u>The Book<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1523282247i/25349507._SY540_.jpg" width="377" height="600" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></u></blockquote>
<br>It's not the first time to read a Screenplay, yet it's the first time to read it in this elegant book format..<br>Clear, with fine arts sometimes, perfect spacing..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1523282247i/25349508.jpg" width="450" height="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>And the notes between the lines, how Rowling's Novel's Writing Magic on describing the characters...<br></b><blockquote>
  <i>“ Blonde Queenie, the most beautiful girl ever to don witches' robes, is standing in a silk slip, supervising the mending of a dress on a dressmaker's dummy. Jacob is thunderstruck. ” <br></i>
</blockquote><b>and even the little extra describing of the story..<br></b><blockquote>
  <i>“ A beat as Queenie drinks the whole story out of Newt's head. She looks both intrigued and saddened. Newt continues to work, trying hard to pretend Queenie isn't reading his mind. ” </i>
</blockquote><b><br>I know it's not like reading a novel... it's just a different experience.<br>And of course because we all want every story of the Wizarding World in the forum of a book.<br><br>Yet I felt bit disappointed that I needed to read the Deleted Scenes including in the script.. but the book only hold the original film script.<br><br>And , amazingly helpful, If you wish to know the technique of writing a Screenplay, this book is really a gem... it includes the glossary of terms used in writing one...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1523282247i/25349509.jpg" width="450" height="450" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So yeah, go Watch the movie, and Read the Screenplay as well.<br><br><b>~~~~~~~~~~~~<blockquote><u>The Verdict</u></blockquote>
<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479407578i/21187572._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="253" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The Screenplay is Fantastic, magically written, even if I see the story simple this first round,</b> -I'm sure that'd change later-<b> yet reading it now... just wow, marvelous.<br><br>Rich World, Rich Characters, good -not huge or great- Conflict, and Fantastically paced for me.<br><br>The thing here is that, unlike Harry Potter movies. Where its original stories suffer injustice simplification in the process of foreign screenwriters. This time the story fit and complete. this time it's totally J.K.Rowling, the best who can write about this magical world..<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479495784i/21198603._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="255" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the same those who made the Potter series Magical Cinematic experience visually, they're here too to make this series Fantastic Cinematic too.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479416613i/21188532._SY540_.jpg" width="450" height="540" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br></b>Thanks A Million for Amazon.co.uk for sending the book in Priority Shipping,though I didn't pay for that. Thank you.<b><br><br>And remember, it's the first part of the 5 parts Prequel to the Saga of the Boy Who Lived.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462476833i/19002927._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="378" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>We Still have Huger for this Story of the Wizarding World...<br></b><br><br>Mohammed Arabey<br>Pre-Ordered 27 April 2016<br>Pre-Reviewed 4 May 2016<br><br>Movie Review 17 Nov. 2016<br></b></span>

<div id="review_2291381984" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2291381984" />
    <a title="Maria" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/77602709-maria"><img alt="Maria" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1519184646p2/77602709.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2291381984?book_show_action=true">Mar 31, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maria" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maria" href="/user/show/77602709-maria">Maria</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2291381984" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14794503395205669467"><b>4</b>/5 Stars ⭐️ ⭐️ ⭐️ ⭐️ <br/><br/><blockquote>“Newt Scamander : "My philosophy is that worrying means you suffer twice.” <br/><br/>― J.K. Rowling, Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them: The Original Screenplay</blockquote><br/><br/>This is not actually a "book" so I can't really write a review about it but I'll say a few words. <br/><br/>This is a beautifully crafted book with amazing illustrations and a fantastic cover. As a graphic designer student, I always appreciate beautiful artwork throughout books. And I also appreciated the credit that was given to t</span>
  <span id="freeText14794503395205669467" style="display:none"><b>4</b>/5 Stars ⭐️ ⭐️ ⭐️ ⭐️ <br /><br /><blockquote>“Newt Scamander : "My philosophy is that worrying means you suffer twice.” <br /><br />― J.K. Rowling, Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them: The Original Screenplay</blockquote><br /><br />This is not actually a "book" so I can't really write a review about it but I'll say a few words. <br /><br />This is a beautifully crafted book with amazing illustrations and a fantastic cover. As a graphic designer student, I always appreciate beautiful artwork throughout books. And I also appreciated the credit that was given to the artists in the back of the book. Even the fonts were mentioned... they might come in handy... hm...<br /><br />Apart from the looks, this is a screenplay. It's exactly what the movie is. I'm a Harry Potter fanatic, fangirl, geek, nerd, I breath it, it's me, YES I AM HARRY POTTER and I always try to CONSUME anything concerning it. So, naturally, I have watched the FBAWTFT movie many times. Naturally. Along with the lines and descriptions of the book I could picture the scenes in my head perfectly. Not because I have watched the movie many times, oh no, because the book was good at describing them, obviously. Obviously.<br /><br />I also adored how we got to see some more hidden thoughts from the characters (THE SHIPS GUYS THE SHIPS) and some more details from the movie. Furthermore, it contained some deleted scenes I didn't expect to see. Nice touch there.<br /><br />In conclusion, this was a little book, I started it 3 hours ago and I just finished and it was a great HP break. I'm considering watching the movie again after this... maybe... hm... And again, till the next one K BYE!</span>
  <a data-text-id="14794503395205669467" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1817734955" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1817734955" />
    <a title="Sean Barrs " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27788046-sean-barrs"><img alt="Sean Barrs " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605281953p2/27788046.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1817734955?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sean Barrs " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sean Barrs " href="/user/show/27788046-sean-barrs">Sean Barrs </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27788046-sean-barrs?shelf=4-star-reads">4-star-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27788046-sean-barrs?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27788046-sean-barrs?shelf=children-of-all-ages">children-of-all-ages</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1817734955" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9818959961370636397">After the travesty known as <i> Harry Potter and The Cursed Child, </i> I really needed this adventure.<br/> <br/>So here are some reasons why it succeeded where <i> The Cursed Child</i> failed:<br/><br/><b>1. It’s actually fun</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478177688ra/21043119.gif' width='400' height='175' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>The Cursed Child is all so very serious. Granted, Harry’s life has some pretty dark moments, though it always foregrounded by this idea of friendship and love. The Cursed child just felt depressing. This carries with it all the whimsical humour of the earlier Harry Potter books before things became dark and </span>
  <span id="freeText9818959961370636397" style="display:none">After the travesty known as <i> Harry Potter and The Cursed Child, </i> I really needed this adventure.<br> <br>So here are some reasons why it succeeded where <i> The Cursed Child</i> failed:<br><br><b>1. It’s actually fun</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478177688ra/21043119.gif" width="400" height="175" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The Cursed Child is all so very serious. Granted, Harry’s life has some pretty dark moments, though it always foregrounded by this idea of friendship and love. The Cursed child just felt depressing. This carries with it all the whimsical humour of the earlier Harry Potter books before things became dark and serious. The plot relayed all the clumsiness members of the wizarding world seem to possess. It made me laugh. <br><br><br><b>2. A great new character </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479733310ra/21228708.gif" width="400" height="175" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479733310ra/21228709.gif" width="400" height="175" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479733310ra/21228710.gif" width="400" height="175" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479733006ra/21228667.gif" width="400" height="175" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Newt Scamander feels like he belongs in this world. He has all the characteristics of the Hufflepuff house, such as dedication and loyalty which are shown in his devotion to his animals. This seems like an obvious things to say, but when considering the fact that half the characters in <i> The Cursed Child </i> felt out of place, it becomes a necessity. He’s also played by one of my favourite actors in the movie; he seems like a perfect cast for the role. <br><br><b>3. Lack of dependency </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479733166ra/21228693.gif" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>This could exist on its own. It's a new story in the normal world. If you’re one of those strange people who have not yet read or watched the Harry Potter series, you’d still easily enjoy this. It does draw on some aspects of the already established universe, but not so much that they define the plot. This felt independent and new. Returning readers will also enjoy the references, but at the same time still be able to enjoy its separateness. <br><br>So this was rather good even in this form. It would have been nice to see it novelised but I suppose the movie is the real thing in question, this is just a fortunate by-product. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="9818959961370636397" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1823573096?book_show_action=true">Dec 02, 2016</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1823573096" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2072913655318499061"><b>
  <u>Magical Experience!</u>
</b><br/><br/><br/><i>This is the screenplay of the film of the same title, don’t confuse with the previously published reference book sharing the same title, and also by J.K. Rowling.</i><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>A NEW(T) HERO IN THE WIZARDING WORLD</u>
</b><br/><br/>If I am dreaming, please don’t wake me! Two new books by J.K. Rowling (this one and <i>Harry Potter and the Cursed Child</i>) plus three digital short stories, expanding the Wizarding World of <i>Harry Potter</i> in the same year! Oh, yeah! Wicked! I couldn’t ask for something better!<br/><br/>The </span>
  <span id="freeText2072913655318499061" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>Magical Experience!</u>
</b><br /><br /><br /><i>This is the screenplay of the film of the same title, don’t confuse with the previously published reference book sharing the same title, and also by J.K. Rowling.</i><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>A NEW(T) HERO IN THE WIZARDING WORLD</u>
</b><br /><br />If I am dreaming, please don’t wake me! Two new books by J.K. Rowling (this one and <i>Harry Potter and the Cursed Child</i>) plus three digital short stories, expanding the Wizarding World of <i>Harry Potter</i> in the same year! Oh, yeah! Wicked! I couldn’t ask for something better!<br /><br />The Wizarding World of J.K. Rowling comes to the Americas finally, using New York City as the scenario of the adventure at hand,…<br /><br />…and I guess that it was something to be happen, sooner or later, but reading in the web about the intentions of using Paris as the next location in this new prequel series, it seems that <i>Harry Potter</i> Magical Universe isn’t only coming to USA, but it will reach eventually the whole world!<br /><br />But, meanwhile, let me tell you about the adventure of this book…<br /><br />…set in 1926, about 70 years before the beginning of the events of the original <i>Harry Potter</i> literary saga.<br /><br />Harry Potter was the central character of the previous book series,…<br /><br />…but now the new central character is <b>
  <u>Newt Scamander</u>
</b>, a young adult British Magizoologist (a wizard with a specialization handling magical creatures), who has been traveling around the whole world, saving magical beasts and keeping them with him, thanks to a magical suitcase (who it's bigger on the inside… British pop culture pun intended!), that it could use better locks…<br /><br />…since soon enough, some of Newt’s magical animals escape into the big city of New York and mayhem will happen…<br /><br />…but there is a secret darkness already in New York, an evil force looking for a powerful being to weaponize it against the whole wizarding community!<br /><br /><br /> <b>
  <u>MUGGLE V. NO-MAJ: DAWN OF NON-MAGIC PEOPLE</u>
</b><br /><br />In this magical adventure, Newt Scamander will find some allies, a couple of witch sisters and…<br /><br />…a muggle!!! Sorry, a No-Maj (well, at least that’s how the American wizards call to the non-magical people there).<br /><br />I think that it’s wonderful to have a Muggle (sorry, habits die hard) as one of the main characters since in the original <i>Harry Potter</i> series, all the main characters were wizards (in the worse case, Squibs (people without magic but still born from wizards)) and the non-magical people were basically tertiary characters with hardly any relevance or dialogues, but here you have…<br /><br />…Jacob Kowalski, potential baker! Oh, yeah!<br /><br />About the witch sisters, the Goldstein sisters, Porpentina aka “Tina”, demoted Auror in MACUSA (Magical Congress of the United States of America), and Queenie, who is a Legilimens (a witch able to read minds).<br /><br />This unlikely quartet is the best chance for New York against dark menaces from different angles, colliding at the same time, in the city that never sleeps…<br /><br />…but a deathly power is awakens…<br /><br />…and nobody will be safe, wizards and mug…mmh…no-majs alike!<br /><br />The Wizarding World of J.K. Rowling just got larger!<br /><br />And we are only just beginning!<br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2072913655318499061" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1815843491" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17530663348517316107">I slept on it. I didn't want to write my review right away because I wanted to see if my feelings would calm down. And they did. A little. Otherwise I still feel a longing for more, some kind of happy sadness (yes, I've gone completely insane).<br/><br/>About 15 minutes after finishing the screenplay, still struggling to control myself, I went to my husband and told him that I really need a physical copy. And not only do I need it, but I <i>want</i> it. And it has to be in English because I don't want any alteri</span>
  <span id="freeText17530663348517316107" style="display:none">I slept on it. I didn't want to write my review right away because I wanted to see if my feelings would calm down. And they did. A little. Otherwise I still feel a longing for more, some kind of happy sadness (yes, I've gone completely insane).<br><br>About 15 minutes after finishing the screenplay, still struggling to control myself, I went to my husband and told him that I really need a physical copy. And not only do I need it, but I <i>want</i> it. And it has to be in English because I don't want any altering to it.<br><br>I strongly recommend that you see the movie first. If by some chance you don't like it (what's wrong with you?), you're not going to like this either. Reading the screenplay feels like rewatching the film in slow motion (because of my reading speed). Also, the cinematic version has exquisite effects that will definitely improve on your imagination. The beast are both adorable and majestic.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479880267ra/21246122.gif" width="500" height="207" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479880459ra/21246139.gif" width="480" height="270" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479880459ra/21246140.gif" width="500" height="259" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479880543ra/21246147.gif" width="600" height="249" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I saw some reviews of people disappointed that this was not a Harry Potter movie. And to that I am speechless. There is no HP in the title and the plot is set way before he was born. So I don't see a connection. What I do see is an amazing movie (with a wonderful screenplay) that stands on its own. Take away all you know about HP and this is still a great movie.<br><br>My absolute favorite character is Jacob, the No-Maj (or Muggle, if you prefer). He's the comic relief, but he's more than a silly character. He's got courage and compassion, and I'm proud that our kind got him depicting us. Jacob brought tears to my eyes, and I love him dearly.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479881490ra/21246273.gif" width="500" height="203" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So, to sum up, go see the movie and get the screenplay. They are both worth it.<br><br>***********************************************<br><br><b>✔ Read Newt Scamander's book.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479804462i/21236823.jpg" width="320" height="493" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>✔ See amazing movie.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479804585i/21236846._SY540_.jpg" width="480" height="594" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>✔ Read movie screenplay.</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479804778i/21236877.jpg" width="321" height="499" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14768394191809772698">Can you IMAGINE being so mind-numbingly in demand that you're offered money to publish a screenplay you were already paid to write, the screenplay for a movie off which you will still profit, a movie which is inspired by a book you already wrote, a book which is actually just a textbook you mentioned in a series that you already completed, a series that has sold hundreds of millions of copies and spawned its own billion-dollar world of movies?<br/><br/>There is straight up no reason for JK Rowling to not </span>
  <span id="freeText14768394191809772698" style="display:none">Can you IMAGINE being so mind-numbingly in demand that you're offered money to publish a screenplay you were already paid to write, the screenplay for a movie off which you will still profit, a movie which is inspired by a book you already wrote, a book which is actually just a textbook you mentioned in a series that you already completed, a series that has sold hundreds of millions of copies and spawned its own billion-dollar world of movies?<br /><br />There is straight up no reason for JK Rowling to not be the richest person in this world. Clearly she doesn't have standards preventing her from publishing anything that will make her money - this book is out in the world, after all.<br /><br />It's not even a book, for god's sake.</span>

<div id="review_1817664092" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1817664092" />
    <a title="P " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25327841-p"><img alt="P " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1489853536p2/25327841.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1817664092?book_show_action=true">Nov 21, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="P " class="user" itemprop="url" name="P " href="/user/show/25327841-p">P </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/30065028-fantastic-beasts-and-where-to-find-them">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25327841-p?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1817664092" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9285142566474040898"><b>
  <blockquote>"Because I like you. Because you’re my friend and I’ll never forget how you helped me, Jacob."</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479838065i/21242941._SX540_.jpg' width='400' height='220' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>First of all, I really loved the design of this book, especially when you just finished those chapters and saw the pictures of each fantastic beast. I couldn't stop myself from rubbing the cover all the time when I held this book in my hands, it was gorgeous and shining as if I was staring at a piece of art, not a book.<br/><br/><b>
  <blockquote>Tell me—has anyone ever believed you when you told them not to worry?</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/>This is </span>
  <span id="freeText9285142566474040898" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>"Because I like you. Because you’re my friend and I’ll never forget how you helped me, Jacob."</blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479838065i/21242941._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="220" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First of all, I really loved the design of this book, especially when you just finished those chapters and saw the pictures of each fantastic beast. I couldn't stop myself from rubbing the cover all the time when I held this book in my hands, it was gorgeous and shining as if I was staring at a piece of art, not a book.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Tell me—has anyone ever believed you when you told them not to worry?</blockquote>
</b><br><br>This is definitely a Rowling's work; it's funny, charming and full of magic. I got goosebumps since I heard Hedwig's theme and the logo of this movie filled the screen. The first page of this book was very spectacular, too.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479838459ra/21243000.gif" width="400" height="180" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Let's move to the story. The book started off with the great potential, which gave me the great vibes of old New York. Newt comes to the city for his secret reason, but he lets his magical creatures escape from his case, that's where things get messy. <br><br>Although everything in Fantastic Beasts didn't cause me to have Harry Potter nostalgia, it still captivated me with the world building and magic system that I was familiar with, such as spells and the differrence between Witches and No-Maj. The political system in this book is intense and mature either. MACUSA in an organisation working as the Minister of Magic in UK and No-Majs stand for Mauggles. I was interested by this side of magic in America.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479838091i/21242942._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>However, Newt is not my favorite character. I'm fond of Credence. His character has a thing to distract me from the hero since I first met him. Credence has been punished for all his deeds without reasons and unfortunately, no one loves him and cares for him, that makes him a stoical child. Ezra slayed this role completely, I was astounded by his countenance and the way he gawks at other people, it was so creepy and amazing at the same time. You know.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479838459ra/21243001.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story is quite slow until the second half. Honesly, I focused on the costumes and soundtrack instead of the story. I think the reason that this happened because the movie couldn't balance two important things, which is the story and the CG, without leaving another thing out.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>My momma, your momma,<br>flying on a switch,<br>My momma, your momma,<br>witches never cry,<br>My momma, your momma,<br>witches gonna die!</blockquote>
</b><br><br>I wasn't excited about those magical creatures, too. I felt kind of so-so for the most part of this movie, maybe it was my false that I expected too much. I mean I liked it but wasn't impressed. This should have been better if Rowling or the producer kept their style as in the Harry Potter series. Those twists. Those plots. Those endings. The narration is kinda straightforward and has nothing to surpirse me, not like HP. I got annoyed so many times by Tina. I didn't like her at all. Her character is boring and not different than annoying heroines from other movies.<br><br>All in all, both the book and movie are still worth waiting and reading. If you are a big fan of Harry Potter, you can't miss this, no matter what.<br><br><b>4 stars for the movie and 3 stars for the book</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479838459i/21243002._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="220" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>More at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://goo.gl/47yHFk">https://goo.gl/47yHFk</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="9285142566474040898" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1839811204" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1839811204" />
    <a title="Mansuriah Hassan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26126450-mansuriah-hassan"><img alt="Mansuriah Hassan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1580314850p2/26126450.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1839811204?book_show_action=true">Dec 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mansuriah Hassan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mansuriah Hassan" href="/user/show/26126450-mansuriah-hassan">Mansuriah Hassan</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/30065028-fantastic-beasts-and-where-to-find-them">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26126450-mansuriah-hassan?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1839811204" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8725892855203529438">I am a <b>HUGE</b> fan of <b>Harry Potter</b>. Even though Harry is not in this story but that doesn't matter because the magic is still beautiful. There are great new characters, story, and of course the fantastic beasts themselves! This is a beautifully published hardback on very nice matte paper with wonderful whimsical line drawings throughout the book. The blue and gold embossed dust jacket is a work of art in itself. For anyone who loves books, this book is a keeper.<br/><br/>This is a screenplay so don't assume </span>
  <span id="freeText8725892855203529438" style="display:none">I am a <b>HUGE</b> fan of <b>Harry Potter</b>. Even though Harry is not in this story but that doesn't matter because the magic is still beautiful. There are great new characters, story, and of course the fantastic beasts themselves! This is a beautifully published hardback on very nice matte paper with wonderful whimsical line drawings throughout the book. The blue and gold embossed dust jacket is a work of art in itself. For anyone who loves books, this book is a keeper.<br /><br />This is a screenplay so don't assume it's a regular novel like the original seven <b>Harry Potter</b> books. I did not read this until after I had seen the movie, so I had the visuals playing in my head as I read, down to Newt's awkwardness and Jacob's wonder. Even without seeing the movie first, this screenplay gives you enough story to be able to appreciate the dangers of this new Wizarding World.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1077326.J_K__Rowling" title="J.K. Rowling" rel="nofollow noopener">J.K. Rowling</a> is a wizard at writing. The story line flows so smoothly and you can picture everything easily in your mind. For those that don't know a lot about stage direction, there is a dictionary of the terms they use in the back, but honestly you'll catch on super quick. Everything is very well detailed and the story will have you turning the page for more and more. I also love how it accurately portrays <b>Hufflepuffs</b>. <br /><br />I finished the book in one sitting and enjoyed the ending so much that I wanted to pick it up again and read from start to finish. All the characters were fresh and adorable. All the beasts were indeed fantastic. I am impatiently looking forward to learning more about <b>Dumbledore</b> and <b>Grindelwald</b>'s past (and about a little secret revealed in this book) in the next movie. Not one bit disappointed. <br /><br />A definite must read if you love the <b>Harry Potter</b> series <b>❤</b><br /><br /><i>“Will we die, just a little?”</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="8725892855203529438" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1747156706?book_show_action=true">Sep 03, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ambsreads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ambsreads" href="/user/show/30813900-ambsreads">ambsreads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781408708989" href="/book/show/30030950-fantastic-beasts-and-where-to-find-them">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=best-covers">best-covers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1747156706" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13389349723665211061"><i>Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them</i> is the screenplay for the movie. I couldn't find a single difference from the movie I watched yesterday. It was such a detailed script which invited you to follow the storyline closely. <br/><br/>The characters are JK Rowling fantastic and so is the storyline. I don't have much else to say, about the characters or the plot, I'm just so in love with this 1926 spin-off of the Harry Potter world. <br/><br/><b>A definite must read if you love the Harry Potter series</b>. </span>

<div id="review_2282209654" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2282209654" />
    <a title="Helena of Eretz ✰" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27036454-helena-of-eretz"><img alt="Helena of Eretz ✰" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1596076376p2/27036454.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2282209654?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Helena of Eretz ✰" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Helena of Eretz ✰" href="/user/show/27036454-helena-of-eretz">Helena of Eretz ✰</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781408708989" href="/book/show/30030950-fantastic-beasts-and-where-to-find-them">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27036454-helena-of-eretz?shelf=hardback">hardback</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27036454-helena-of-eretz?shelf=childrens">childrens</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27036454-helena-of-eretz?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27036454-helena-of-eretz?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2282209654" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13590542484691969425">I’m not going to lie…I’m still <b>rather bitter</b> that J.K. Rowling has decided to release <b>only the scripts</b>, rather than taking a little bit more time to <i>develop them</i> into full-length novels, but I guess this assures that nothing shall be cut from the book when the film is made??? <br/><br/>Either way, this is one of the attributing factors that has caused J.K. Rowling to take a <b>nosedive</b> down my <i>Favourite Authors</i> list. If <b>Cassandra Clare, Holly Black, and Leigh Bardugo</b> can keep expanding their created worlds, </span>
  <span id="freeText13590542484691969425" style="display:none">I’m not going to lie…I’m still <b>rather bitter</b> that J.K. Rowling has decided to release <b>only the scripts</b>, rather than taking a little bit more time to <i>develop them</i> into full-length novels, but I guess this assures that nothing shall be cut from the book when the film is made??? <br><br>Either way, this is one of the attributing factors that has caused J.K. Rowling to take a <b>nosedive</b> down my <i>Favourite Authors</i> list. If <b>Cassandra Clare, Holly Black, and Leigh Bardugo</b> can keep expanding their created worlds, why can’t she? I guess I just don’t love J.K. Rowling as much as I once did anymore. Maybe it’s because <i>I’ve gotten older</i> and have read the works of much better authors, or maybe it’s because of the kinds of <i>things she’s said</i> that makes the news on a regular basis…which have <b>altered my opinion</b> of her. Regardless, I don’t rush to get my hands on anything Harry Potter-related anymore, which as a self-proclaimed <b>Potterhead</b>, <i>breaks my heart</i>. If you could see my room, you’d see Gryffindor merchandise everywhere (<i>YES! GRYFFINDOR AND PROUD!</i>) and an entire bookshelf devoted to <i>special editions</i> of the Harry Potter series that were <b>even imported</b> to add to my collection, along with a number of adorable FunKo Pops. <br><br>It made me <b>so happy</b> to add a new book to my Harry Potter shelf after <i>SO MANY YEARS</i> (Don’t get me started on the fact that after <i>YEARS</i> of fans asking for it, we <i>STILL</i> don’t have a Marauders’ series in the works, yet J.K. Rowling <i>STILL</i> finds ways to milk the Harry Potter universe by re-releasing the books <b>over and over again</b>, every bloody year). Despite my disappointment at a <b>seemingly random</b> film series, I did end up <b>loving the heck</b> out of this script. But does there really need to be <i>five instalments</i>???<br><br>I rarely go to the cinema, as I prefer books to film, so I <b>devoured</b> this script long before I ever saw the film. In fact, I saw the film <i>maybe a week</i> before it left the cinema. (Going to the movies is expensive, ok?!!! I spend all my money on books!!!) <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468247919ra/19683415.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I’m <i>not a fan</i> of <b>Johnny Depp</b> as <b>Grindelwald</b> because I’ve been envisioning the character as an older <b>Jamie Campbell-Bower</b>, who portrayed him in the Harry Potter films…and because it’s been quite some time since Johnny Depp has been in a good movie. I didn’t want his <i>lacklustre performance</i> to <b>affect the overall quality</b> of the Fantastic Beasts film. After seeing the film…yep, my opinion of him <b>hasn’t changed</b> <i>at all</i> LOL. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1549238959ra/27011260.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Newt Scamander</b> was an <i>adorable Hufflepuff</i> and I <b>absolutely loved him</b>. Seriously…I would <i>DIE</i> for him. What an absolute cutie. <b>Eddie Redmayne</b> was <i>PERFECT</i>. Don’t get me wrong; he was great in <i>Les Misèrables</i>, but <i>here</i> was where he really shined. I thought that the <i>main plot</i> was complete and utter <i>FUN</i> as we chased around Manhattan, in search of the <b>escaped creatures</b> who freed themselves from Newt’s case. Newt was such a <b>wonderful caretaker</b> who truly <b>loved his creatures</b>, even humanising them by attaching very human names to them, such as Frank and Dougal. When he was in trouble, Newt’s <b>first concern</b> was his creatures. And when they went missing around the city, he was so worried because they were lost, surrounded by <b>vicious humans</b>, and that’s completely valid. Animals respect other animal species, but humans have always viewed animals as <i>lesser creatures</i>, considering them to be below us, even though dolphins – for example – are a more intelligent species.<br><br>The <i>subplot</i> about the <b>rise of Grindelwald</b> <i>wasn’t as interesting</i> to me. <b>Queenie and Tina</b> were absolute sweethearts, especially Queenie. I’ve always been fascinated by <b>Legilimens</b> and seeing it used by Queenie was riveting. I’d totally kill for that ability more than any other one, haha. <b>Credence</b> was also really cute, and I <i>hated</i> what happened to him. Damn you, Grindelwald!!! <i>Grrr</i>…<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1483986978ra/21669087.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I also loved seeing the wizarding world through <b>Jacob</b>’s eyes because although we’ve seen <i>Muggleborns</i> in the past, we never really got to know any <i>Muggles</i> (in a positive sense, let’s not count the Dursleys) in the Harry Potter series. His story arc also made me rather <b>sad</b>, because although Jacob was <i>with them</i>, he was never truly <i>one of them</i>, which is <b>how I’ve always felt</b>, since I never received my Hogwarts letter. I felt like I was <i>with</i> Harry, Ron, Hermione, Luna, Ginny, and Neville as I read the books, but I never had the opportunity to <i>take part in the magic</i>. I lived vicariously through them and had to <b>imagine</b> what attending Hogwarts would’ve been like. <br><br>My <i>favourite creatures</i> were definitely:<br><br>the <b>Niffler</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1479928677ra/21253453.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and the <b>Bowtruckle</b>, <i>Pickett</i>, in particular.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1549238959ra/27011261.gif" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I <b>can’t wait</b> to see more of Newt, Pickett, Queenie, Tina, and Jacob in the next film!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13590542484691969425" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2555463085" />
    <a title="Mary S. R." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/75831724-mary-s-r"><img alt="Mary S. R." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1597037601p2/75831724.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2555463085?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mary S. R." class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mary S. R." href="/user/show/75831724-mary-s-r">Mary S. R.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75831724-mary-s-r?shelf=faves">faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75831724-mary-s-r?shelf=humor">humor</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75831724-mary-s-r?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75831724-mary-s-r?shelf=historical-fiction">historical-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75831724-mary-s-r?shelf=adult">adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2555463085" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14503334655621110036"><b>5 BEAST-SIZED STARS!</b> funny, adorable, thrilling, and unputdownable.<blockquote>
  <i>“My philosophy is that worrying means you suffer twice.”</i>
</blockquote><b>A screenplay with rich world building and a gripping, hilarious plot</b> (NOT a novel! The format is <i>very</i> different) written by J.K. Rowling (it's not like the Cursed Child).<br/><br/>In <i>Fantastic Beasts</i>, we follow the fictional character and author of the original <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30652372.Fantastic_Beasts_and_Where_to_Find_Them__Hogwarts_Library_' title='Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them (Hogwarts Library) by J.K. Rowling' rel='nofollow noopener'> Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them</a>, the geeky Newt Scamander, as he looks for magical creatures and gets sucked int</span>
  <span id="freeText14503334655621110036" style="display:none"><b>5 BEAST-SIZED STARS!</b> funny, adorable, thrilling, and unputdownable.<blockquote>
  <i>“My philosophy is that worrying means you suffer twice.”</i>
</blockquote><b>A screenplay with rich world building and a gripping, hilarious plot</b> (NOT a novel! The format is <i>very</i> different) written by J.K. Rowling (it's not like the Cursed Child).<br><br>In <i>Fantastic Beasts</i>, we follow the fictional character and author of the original <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30652372.Fantastic_Beasts_and_Where_to_Find_Them__Hogwarts_Library_" title="Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them (Hogwarts Library) by J.K. Rowling" rel="nofollow noopener"> Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them</a>, the geeky Newt Scamander, as he looks for magical creatures and gets sucked into a war he'd not really cared to participate in.<blockquote>“People are easiest to read when they're hurting.”</blockquote>With a “Glossary of Film Terms” at the end, you'd have no problem whatsoever in enjoying <b>this enchanting piece of art.</b> Not to talk about the <i>illustrations</i>! Like these:<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550420791i/27080327._SY540_.jpg" height="124" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550420791i/27080328._SY540_.jpg" height="124" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550420791i/27080329._SY540_.jpg" height="124" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550420791i/27080330._SY540_.jpg" height="124" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>
  <b>Storyline</b>
</u><blockquote>Tina: Mr. Scamander, do you know <i>anything</i> about the wizarding community in America?<br><br>Newt: I do know a few things, actually. I know you have rather backwards laws about relations with non-magic people. That you're not meant to befriend them, that you can't marry them, which seems mildly absurd to me.</blockquote><b>1926, New York.</b><br>Newt Scamander, magizoologist and aspiring author, has come to America for the book he is writing about understanding the mostly-assumed-dangerous and misunderstood magical creatures which wizards say should be killed.<blockquote>
  <i>“See, they're currently in alien terrain, surrounded by millions of the most vicious creatures on the planet. Humans.”</i>
</blockquote>He is carrying a <b>case filled with unimaginable beasts</b> ... when disaster strikes and the creatures are set loose in the city!<blockquote>“My momma, your momma,<br>gonna catch a witch,<br>My momma, your momma,<br>flying on a switch,<br>My momma, your momma,<br>witches never cry,<br>My momma, your momma,<br>witches gonna die!”</blockquote>But there are <s>Muggles</s>—no, No-Majs—who call themselves Second Salemers and believe wizards exist, wanting to make the people aware and warn them of these abominations.<blockquote>“Will we die, just a little?”</blockquote>But <b>with dark magic on the horizon and the Global Wizarding War a stone's throw away, there might be something else happening behind the curtains...</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550481618i/27082766._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>
  <b>Characterization</b>
</u><br><br>• <i>
  <b>Newt Scamander:</b>
</i> an English wizard, a Magizoologist, and a Hufflepuff, he graduated from Hogwarts and joined the Ministry of Magic, spending two years in the Office for House-Elf Relocation before joining the Beast Division. In 1918 he was commissioned by Augustus Worme of Obscurus Books to write <i>Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them</i>. Now, in the last stages of writing his book, he finds himself in America for magical-creature-related business.<br><br>Dedicated, tireless, reasonable, geeky, awkward around people but comfortable with beasts, <b>he is the furthest thing from Harry Potter</b>; though he shares his compassion, special kind of strength, and the tendency to stand up for what's right. <b>Newt made this whole story adorable and gave it a memorable flare</b> :) major props to the lovely Hufflepuffs!<br><br><br>• <i>
  <b>Porpentina Esther “Tina” Goldstein:</b>
</i> a half-blooded American witch who graduated from <i>Ilvermony</i> (the American school of witchcraft and wizardry, where she was sorted into the <i>Thunderbird</i> house) and works for the <i>Magical Congress of the United States of America</i> (MACUSA) as an auror.<br><br>Practical, level-headed, and grounded, she's very soulful, courageous, ambitious, and <b>has a desire to stand up for what is right</b>. I <i>love</i> these about her!<br><br><br>• <i>
  <b>Queenie Goldstein:</b>
</i> an accomplished Legilimens—someone with the ability to extract feelings and memories from another’s mind—and a half-blood American witch, she attended <i>Ilvermorny School of Witchcraft and Wizardry</i>, where she was sorted into <i>Pukwudgie</i> house.<br><br>She has desk job in the Wand Permit Office, within the <i>Magical Congress of the United States of America</i>.<br><br>There's more to her than what you get at the first glance; Queenie's free-spirited, kind-hearted, empathic, compassionate, and very brave. I'm really intrigued to see where her character goes in the series :))<br><br><br>• <i>
  <b>Jacob Kowalski:</b>
</i> a Polish-born American No-Maj (non-wizard), Jacob fought in the First World War. Returning home to the United States he found work in a cannery, but dreamt of becoming a baker—and it was that dream that changed his life when he went to the bank for a loan...<br><br>I <i>love</i> this guy! <b>It's amazing that there's a proper Muggle as a protagonist</b> (unlike Harry Potter) and seeing him react to magic was interesting! He's so <b>lovable and adaptable</b>, extremely warm, welcoming, compassionate, and friendly, he wants to make people happy and I just wanna hug him :)<blockquote>Jacob: Newt...I don't think I'm dreaming.<br>Newt <i>(vaguely amused)</i>: What gave it away?<br>Jacob: I ain't got the brains to make this up.</blockquote>• <i>
  <b>Magical creatures:</b>
</i> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550456224i/27081806.jpg" height="30" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They were probably <b>my favourite thing</b> about this installment, and they make me <i>really</i> wish this had been a novel—because we could've explored their characteristics more thoroughly!<br>Though, there's still the original <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30652372.Fantastic_Beasts_and_Where_to_Find_Them__Hogwarts_Library_" title="Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them (Hogwarts Library) by J.K. Rowling" rel="nofollow noopener"> Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them</a> which can help you!<br><br>But even in these short few pages, <b>their personalities were beautifully built</b>; like Pickett, the loyal and sneaky little Bowtruckle with attachment issues<br><br><u>A list of the ones included:</u> Niffler (<i>I want one!</i>), House Elf, Occamy (<i>incredible</i>), Murtlap, Billywig, Swooping Evil (<i>the best!</i>), Thunderbird (<i>glorious</i>), Giant Dung Beetles (<i>hilarious while in the background rolling dung</i>), Graphorns, Fwooper, Bowtruckle (<i>I need one!! please!</i>), Nundu (<i>wow</i>), Doxy, Glow Bug, Grindylow, Diricrawl, Mooncalf (<i>oh man, I love this one so much I just wanna eat it—nooo, that sounds horrible. I don't actually wanna eat it, it's so cute I wanna squeez it—wait, no, let's just say I'd like to tenderly hug it and then kindly pat it...</i>), Mirmite (<i>mesmerising</i>), Obscurus (<i>dark and intriguing</i>), Erumpent (<i>its mating dance was my undoing!</i>), Goblin, Giant, Ashwinder Egg, and Demiguise (<i>my adorable whitebeard</i>).<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550421934i/27080368._SY540_.jpg" height="115" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550421934i/27080369._SX540_.jpg" height="115" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550421934i/27080370._SY540_.jpg" height="115" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550421934i/27080371._SX540_.jpg" height="115" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550422671i/27080438._SY540_.jpg" height="110" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550422672i/27080440._SY540_.jpg" height="110" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550422672i/27080441._SY540_.jpg" height="110" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1550422672i/27080439._SX540_.jpg" height="110" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>
  <b>Movie Adaptation</b>
</u><br><br><i>
  <b>Casting &amp; Acting:</b>
</i> Just imagine what a hard thing it is to play in a movie that's got a magical creature in every other scene, and not just <i>there</i> as decoration but for you to constantly interact with—including feeding, patting, chastising, talking to, chasing, or even doing mating dance to!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1550455324ra/27081752.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>You have to look at a stick—or nothing—and just imagine a creature that doesn't even <i>exist</i> really and one you've never met or will meet. Every bit of imagination will be squeezed out of the actor at the end of the day, leaving an exhausted shell—<b>so, well done! The acting was just impressive.</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1550455324ra/27081753.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Eddie Redmayne (<i>Newt Scamander</i>) was the <i>perfect</i> guy for the job! He was practically glowing in this adaptation. I have long been a fan and loved that man :) I couldn't be happier that he's been cast, and nor can I imagine anyone else as Newt.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1550455324ra/27081754.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Katherine Waterston (<i>Tina Goldstein</i>), however, a little disappointed me in the acting part and I didn't feel satisfied. I'm still not sure about the choice.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1550455324ra/27081755.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Dan Fogler (<i>Jacob Kowalski</i>) was <i>spectacular</i>. Like, <i>wow</i>! Diving onto the cute confused but enthusiastic Muggle thrown into the Wizarding World without a blink. I enjoyed every <i>single</i> one of his scenes, amd it was a good thing he was usually there!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1550455324ra/27081756.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Alison Sudol (<i>Queenie Goldstein</i>) was another amazing one. Hilarious and flirty and weird, she performed the <i>best</i> Queenie I could hope for!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1550458434ra/27081879.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ezra Miller (<i>Credence Barebone</i>) also <i>slayed</i> the role of the abused and sensitive child! My heart broke for him and Miller just got to me with the precious acting :)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1550458434ra/27081880.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>
  <b>Directing, CGI, etc:</b>
</i> David Yates (who also directed the final for films of Harry Potter) did such an awesome job with <i>Fantastic Beasts and Where to Find Them</i>. The production was just <i>mesmerising</i> and I was in <i>awe</i> of the special effects and magical creatures. I was just lost! Some of my faves:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1550455324ra/27081757.gif" height="76" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1550458434ra/27081881.gif" height="76" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1550458434ra/27081882.gif" height="81" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1550458434ra/27081883.gif" height="81" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><u>
  <b>Companions</b>
</u><br><br><i>
  <b>Books in series:</b>
</i><br>• <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/39330961.Fantastic_Beasts_The_Crimes_of_Grindelwald___The_Original_Screenplay" title="Fantastic Beasts The Crimes of Grindelwald - The Original Screenplay by J.K. Rowling" rel="nofollow noopener"> Fantastic Beasts: The Crimes of Grindelwald - The Original Screenplay</a> (Fantastic Beasts The Original Screenplay, #2) [<b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2556973638" rel="nofollow noopener">MY REVIEW</a>
</b>]<br><br><i>
  <b>Related books:</b>
</i><br>• <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22841994.Harry_Potter_and_the_Philosopher_s_Stone__Harry_Potter__1_" title="Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone (Harry Potter #1) by J.K. Rowling" rel="nofollow noopener"> Harry Potter and the Philosopher's Stone</a> (Harry Potter, #1)<br>• <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22841998.Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets__Harry_Potter___2_" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets (Harry Potter, #2) by J.K.   <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1812558932" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1812558932?book_show_action=true">Nov 25, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Eleanne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Eleanne" href="/user/show/39657117-eleanne">Eleanne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781408708989" href="/book/show/30030950-fantastic-beasts-and-where-to-find-them">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1812558932" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15335875045203957260"><b>FIRST OF ALL! CAN SOMEONE TELL ME HOW CAN I TRAVEL THROUGH TIME AND MARRY NEWT SCAMANDER???</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1376.photobucket.com/user/Ely_GV/media/tumblr_oh66h3vBSQ1tlman9o5_500_zps9duzva2s.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480073032ra/21270945.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_oh66h3vBSQ1tlman9o5_500_zps9duzva2s.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>He's so dreamy and cute! *sighs*</i><br/><br/><a href='http://s1376.photobucket.com/user/Ely_GV/media/tumblr_oh5qeoq5Qj1t2eehqo1_500_zps9fpvc0sp.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480073032ra/21270946.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_oh5qeoq5Qj1t2eehqo1_500_zps9fpvc0sp.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>And he has the most wonderful creatures!<br/><br/><a href='http://s1376.photobucket.com/user/Ely_GV/media/tumblr_oh5qeoq5Qj1t2eehqo2_1280_zpsefbru2um.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480073032ra/21270947.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_oh5qeoq5Qj1t2eehqo2_1280_zpsefbru2um.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>I MELT...</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1376.photobucket.com/user/Ely_GV/media/tumblr_ogwg7qmcRJ1tr15yio1_500_zpsqxawkhb8.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480073032ra/21270948.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_ogwg7qmcRJ1tr15yio1_500_zpsqxawkhb8.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I spent 50% of the movie declaring my love for Newt; 15% swooning over his fantastic beasts; 15% saying this movie was perfection; 15% praising J.K Rowling -I love her so much!!!- and the last 15% was all me fangirling over Queenie. She's my hero. <br/><br/><s>That was 110%. oops. Sorry!</s><br/><br/><a href='http://s1376.photobucket.com/user/Ely_GV/media/tumblr_oh5pyy1o311rszoo3o6_r1_540_zpsixnj3flc.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480073032ra/21270949.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_oh5pyy1o311rszoo3o6_r1_540_zpsixnj3flc.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>By the end of the movie, I was Pi</span>
  <span id="freeText15335875045203957260" style="display:none"><b>FIRST OF ALL! CAN SOMEONE TELL ME HOW CAN I TRAVEL THROUGH TIME AND MARRY NEWT SCAMANDER???</b><br><br><a href="http://s1376.photobucket.com/user/Ely_GV/media/tumblr_oh66h3vBSQ1tlman9o5_500_zps9duzva2s.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480073032ra/21270945.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_oh66h3vBSQ1tlman9o5_500_zps9duzva2s.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>He's so dreamy and cute! *sighs*</i><br><br><a href="http://s1376.photobucket.com/user/Ely_GV/media/tumblr_oh5qeoq5Qj1t2eehqo1_500_zps9fpvc0sp.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480073032ra/21270946.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_oh5qeoq5Qj1t2eehqo1_500_zps9fpvc0sp.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And he has the most wonderful creatures!<br><br><a href="http://s1376.photobucket.com/user/Ely_GV/media/tumblr_oh5qeoq5Qj1t2eehqo2_1280_zpsefbru2um.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480073032ra/21270947.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_oh5qeoq5Qj1t2eehqo2_1280_zpsefbru2um.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>I MELT...</b><br><br><a href="http://s1376.photobucket.com/user/Ely_GV/media/tumblr_ogwg7qmcRJ1tr15yio1_500_zpsqxawkhb8.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I spent 50% of the movie declaring my love for Newt; 15% swooning over his fantastic beasts; 15% saying this movie was perfection; 15% praising J.K Rowling -I love her so much!!!- and the last 15% was all me fangirling over Queenie. She's my hero. <br><br><s>That was 110%. oops. Sorry!</s><br><br><a href="http://s1376.photobucket.com/user/Ely_GV/media/tumblr_oh5pyy1o311rszoo3o6_r1_540_zpsixnj3flc.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480073032ra/21270949.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_oh5pyy1o311rszoo3o6_r1_540_zpsixnj3flc.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>By the end of the movie, I was Pickett, the Bowtruckle. I really didn't want to leave...<br><br><a href="http://s1376.photobucket.com/user/Ely_GV/media/tumblr_ogsyh17Iwl1rszoo3o5_r1_540_zpsajaevlx6.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1480073032ra/21270950.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_ogsyh17Iwl1rszoo3o5_r1_540_zpsajaevlx6.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Conclusion: I wanna watch it again and again and again. ❤ Even better, I might end up reading it and reading it over and over again.</span>
